[30;1m2 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35m`libtmux` is a [typed](https://docs.python.org/3/library/typing.html) Python library that provides a[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35msessions, windows, and panes. Additionally, `libtmux` powers [tmuxp], a tmux workspace manager.[0m
